/* full width at bottom */\n const rWTop = W * 0.12; /* narrow strip at horizon */\n\n /* Helper: get road left/right X at screen Y */\n function roadEdge(screenY){\n const t = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, (screenY - hY) / (H - hY)));\n const half = rWTop/2 + (rWBot/2 - rWTop/2) * t;\n return { left: W/2 - half, right: W/2 + half, half };\n }\n\n /* \u2500\u2500\u2500 1. SKY / BACKGROUND \u2500\u2500 */\n if(_bgImg && _bgImg.complete && _bgImg.naturalWidth > 0){\n /* Draw nature background image, cropped to top portion */\n ctx.drawImage(_bgImg, 0, 0, W, hY + 20);\n /* Darken bottom of bg to blend into road */\n const blend = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, hY - 40, 0, hY + 20);\n blend.addColorStop(0, 'transparent');\n blend.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.6)');\n ctx.fillStyle = blend;\n ctx.fillRect(0, hY - 40, W, 60);\n } else {\n /* Fallback gradient sky */\n const skyG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, hY);\n skyG.addColorStop(0, '#3a6186');\n skyG.addColorStop(0.6, '#89a0b8');\n skyG.addColorStop(1, '#b5c8d6');\n ctx.fillStyle = skyG;\n ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, hY);\n }\n\n /* \u2500\u2500\u2500 2. ROAD SHOULDER (gravel/grass on sides) \u2500\u2500 */\n {\n const edgeBot = roadEdge(H);\n const edgeHor = roadEdge(hY);\n /* Left shoulder */\n ctx.beginPath();\n ctx.moveTo(0, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeHor.left, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeBot.left, H);\n ctx.lineTo(0, H);\n ctx.closePath();\n const sgL = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, hY, 0, H);\n sgL.addColorStop(0, '#5a7a3a');\n sgL.addColorStop(1, '#3d5c28');\n ctx.fillStyle = sgL;\n ctx.fill();\n /* Right shoulder */\n ctx.beginPath();\n ctx.moveTo(W, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeHor.right, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeBot.right, H);\n ctx.lineTo(W, H);\n ctx.closePath();\n ctx.fillStyle = sgL;\n ctx.fill();\n }\n\n /* \u2500\u2500\u2500 3. ROAD SURFACE \u2500\u2500 */\n {\n const edgeBot = roadEdge(H);\n const edgeHor = roadEdge(hY);\n ctx.beginPath();\n ctx.moveTo(edgeHor.left, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeHor.right, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeBot.right, H);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeBot.left, H);\n ctx.closePath();\n const roadG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, hY, 0, H);\n roadG.addColorStop(0, '#6b6b6b');\n roadG.addColorStop(0.4, '#555555');\n roadG.addColorStop(1, '#404040');\n ctx.fillStyle = roadG;\n ctx.fill();\n }\n\n /* \u2500\u2500\u2500 4. ROAD EDGE LINES (white solid lines) \u2500\u2500 */\n {\n const edgeBot = roadEdge(H);\n const edgeHor = roadEdge(hY);\n ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.85)';\n ctx.lineWidth = 3;\n /* Left edge */\n ctx.beginPath();\n ctx.moveTo(edgeHor.left, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeBot.left, H);\n ctx.stroke();\n /* Right edge */\n ctx.beginPath();\n ctx.moveTo(edgeHor.right, hY);\n ctx.lineTo(edgeBot.right, H);\n ctx.stroke();\n }\n\n /* \u2500\u2500\u2500 5. CENTER DASHED LANE DIVIDER \u2500\u2500 */\n /* We project dashes from world space to screen using perspective.\n World depth increases toward horizon.\n dashSpacing = world units between dashes.\n scrollY acts as camera z offset to scroll dashes. */\n {\n const NUM_STEPS = 200; /* resolution of perspective projection */\n const DASH_PERIOD = 14; /* how many steps per dash+gap */\n const DASH_ON = 6; /* dash \"on\" steps */\n\n ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.80)';\n\n let lastX = W/2;\n let lastY = H;\n let drawing = false;\n\n for(let i = 0; i < NUM_STEPS; i++){\n /* t goes from 0 (bottom of road) to 1 (horizon) */\n const t = i / NUM_STEPS;\n const screenY = H - t * (H - hY);\n\n /* perspective-correct line width */\n const e = roadEdge(screenY);\n const lw = Math.max(1, (1 - t) * 4 + 1);\n\n /* scrolled dash pattern */\n const dashPhase = (i + Math.floor(scrollY * 0.45)) % DASH_PERIOD;\n const isOn = dashPhase < DASH_ON;\n\n if(isOn && !drawing){\n ctx.beginPath();\n ctx.lineWidth = lw;\n ctx.moveTo(W/2, screenY);\n drawing = true;\n } else if(!isOn && drawing){\n ctx.lineTo(W/2, screenY);\n ctx.stroke();\n drawing = false;\n }\n }\n if(drawing){\n ctx.lineTo(W/2, hY);\n ctx.stroke();\n }\n }\n\n /* \u2500\u2500\u2500 6. LANE POSITION MARKERS (white blocks near bottom) \u2500\u2500 */\n {\n /* Small perspective-accurate marks on left and right thirds */\n const MARK_PERIOD = 30;\n const MARK_ON = 10;\n ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)';\n for(let i = 0; i < 60; i++){\n const t = i / 60;\n const screenY = H - t * (H - hY);\n const e = roadEdge(screenY);\n const phase = (i + Math.floor(scrollY * 0.3)) % MARK_PERIOD;\n if(phase < MARK_ON){\n const markH = Math.max(1, (1-t)*3);\n const quarter = (e.right - e.left) / 4;\n ctx.fillRect(e.left + quarter - 1, screenY, 2, markH);\n ctx.fillRect(e.right - quarter - 1, screenY, 2, markH);\n }\n }\n }\n\n /* \u2500\u2500\u2500 7. FINISH LINE BANNER \u2500\u2500 */\n if(finishVisible && finishProgress > 0){\n /* finishProgress 0=at horizon \u2192 1=at camera bottom */\n const fp = Math.min(1, finishProgress);\n const bannerY = hY + fp * (H - hY) * 0.72;\n const e = roadEdge(bannerY);\n const bW = e.right - e.left;\n const bH = Math.max(6, bW * 0.12);\n\n if(_finishImg && _finishImg.complete && _finishImg.naturalWidth > 0){\n /* Draw finish image stretched across road width */\n ctx.drawImage(_finishImg, e.left, bannerY - bH, bW, bH * 1.6);\n } else {\n /* Fallback drawn finish banner */\n const colsF = 12;\n const cWF = bW / colsF;\n for(let c = 0; c < colsF; c++){\n for(let r = 0; r < 2; r++){\n ctx.fillStyle = (c + r) % 2 === 0 ? '#fff' : '#111';\n ctx.fillRect(e.left + c * cWF, bannerY - bH + r * bH/2, cWF, bH/2);\n }\n }\n /* FINISH text */\n const fSize = Math.max(10, bH * 0.9);\n ctx.font = `bold ${fSize}px Fredoka, sans-serif`;\n ctx.fillStyle = '#cc0000';\n ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n ctx.fillText('FINISH', W/2, bannerY - bH/4);\n ctx.textBaseline = 'alphabetic';\n /* Poles */\n ctx.strokeStyle = '#888';\n ctx.lineWidth = Math.max(2, (1-fp)*4);\n ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(e.left, bannerY - bH * 2);ctx.lineTo(e.left, H);ctx.stroke();\n ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(e.right, bannerY - bH * 2);ctx.lineTo(e.right, H);ctx.stroke();\n }\n }\n }\n\n /* \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n CAROUSEL INIT\n \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550 */\n window._raceInit = function(){\n /* Update floating topbar (avatar + name + ton balance) */\n try{\n const av=document.getElementById('raceAvatar');\n const nm=document.getElementById('raceUserName');\n const tb=document.getElementById('raceTonBal');\n if(S && S.user){\n const photoUrl = S.user.photoUrl||(S?.tg?.initDataUnsafe?.user?.photo_url)||null;\n if(av && photoUrl) av.innerHTML = `\ud83c\udfcd\ufe0f'\">`;\n if(nm) nm.textContent = S.user.firstName||S._tgName||'Player';\n if(tb) tb.textContent = (S.user.tonBalance||0).toFixed(4);\n }\n }catch(e){}\n\n _raceBikes = [];\n if(S && S.user && S.user.ownedBikes && S.user.ownedBikes.length > 0){\n S.user.ownedBikes.forEach(lv=>{\n const b = BIKES.find(x=>x.lv===lv);\n if(b && !isBikeMiningActive(lv)) _raceBikes.push(b);\n });\n }\n const track = document.getElementById('raceCarouselTrack');\n if(!track) return;\n const sf = document.getElementById('raceStartFixed');\n if(sf) sf.style.display = 'block';\n if(_raceBikes.length === 0){\n track.innerHTML = '
